  <title>EX-99.1</title>
 </head>
 <body style="margin: auto!important;padding: 8px;line-height: 1;">
  <div style="padding-top:0.5in;z-index:-3;min-height:0.5in;position:relative;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Exhibit 99.1</font></p></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><img src="img17863145_0.jpg" alt="img17863145_0.jpg" style="width:172px;height:48px;"></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:18pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">LM Funding America, Inc. Reports Financial Results and Provides Business Update for the Third Quarter of 2024</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:14pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:14pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Conference Call to Be Held Today at 11:00 am ET</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">TAMPA, FL, November 13, 2024&#x2014;LM Funding America, Inc. (NASDAQ: LMFA) (&#x201c;LM Funding&#x201d; or the &#x201c;Company&#x201d;),</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> a cryptocurrency mining and technology-based specialty finance company, today provided a business update and reported financial results for the three and nine months ended September 30, 2024.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Financial highlights</font></p>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:6pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Held 142.3 Bitcoin on September 30, 2024, Valued at Approximately $12.4 Million Based on Recent Bitcoin Price of $87,000</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Digital mining cost of revenues (exclusive of depreciation and amortization) as a percentage of digital mining revenues showed substantial improvement versus the prior year quarter.</font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">CEO commentary</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Bruce Rodgers, Chairman and CEO of LM Funding, remarked, &#34;Following the April halving event, we initiated a vertical integration strategy, focusing on locations with low-cost power and strong expansion potential. We are committed to identifying cost-effective sites that will enable the Company to drive growth and increase shareholder value. Additionally, we are excited to see Bitcoin recently reach an all-time high above $87,000&#x2014;a milestone that reinforces our strategy of mining and holding Bitcoin as the price approaches the market  projection target of over $100,000 by 2025.&#34;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Strategic Developments</font></p>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Vertical Integration Strategy:</font><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> Following the halving event, the Company transitioned from an infrastructure-light approach to a vertical integration strategy. This shift, strategically coordinated with the expiration of hosting contracts, allowed the Company to secure lower-cost power sources ($0.3 - 0.5 cents per MW) and relocate miners to more cost-effective operations and expansion opportunities. This resulted in gross mining margin improvements to 35% for the quarter as comparted to 18% in the prior year.</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Leadership Appointment:</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> Ryan Duran has been named president of US Digital Mining and Hosting Co LLC, a subsidiary. Duran will play a pivotal role in shaping the strategic direction and optimizing operational efficiency, positioning LM Funding at the forefront of the rapidly evolving cryptocurrency industry.</font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Ryan Duran, President of USDM, stated, &#34;I look forward to driving our vertical integration strategy as we acquire cost-effective sites to lower our operating costs.&#34;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div class="page-node-content"><div style="z-index:-3;flex-direction:column;display:flex;padding-bottom:0.5in;min-height:0.5in;justify-content:flex-end;position:relative;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">1</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p></div></div>
  <hr style="margin-inline-start:auto;margin-inline-end:auto;page-break-after:always;">
  <div style="padding-top:0.5in;z-index:-3;min-height:0.5in;position:relative;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Exhibit 99.1</font></p></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Quarterly Operational Highlights &#x2013; Three Months ended September 30, 2024</font></p>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:3pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Bitcoin Mining:</font><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> Mined 18.5 Bitcoins in Q3 2024, generating approximately $1.1 million in revenue at an average Bitcoin price of $60,870.</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:3pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Bitcoin Holdings:</font><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> As of September 30, 2024, the Company held 142.3 Bitcoins valued at approximately $12.4 million based on a price of $87,000 on November 11, 2024.</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:3pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Revenue Impact:</font><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> Total revenue for the third quarter of 2024 was approximately $1.3 million, a decrease of $2.1 million from the same period last year, primarily due to the anticipated effects of the April 2024 Bitcoin halving event and the transition of our mining machines to a new hosting site.</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:3pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net Loss:</font><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> The net loss for the third quarter was $4.8 million compared to a net loss of $4.7 million for the comparable quarter in 2023.</font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Quarterly Financial Highlights - Three Months ended September 30, 2024</font></p>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Revenue:</font><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> Digital mining revenue decreased to $1.1 million in Q3 2024 from $3.3 million in Q3 2023, despite an increase in Bitcoin prices, due to reduced mined volume arising from the halving event and the repositioning of miners during the quarter.</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Operating Expenses:</font><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> Operating expenses decreased to $5.7 million from $6.6 million year-on-year, due primarily to a decrease in digital mining costs in Bitcoin fair value offset in part by an increase in depreciation and amortization costs. </font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net Loss:</font><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> LM Funding reported a net loss attributable to shareholders of approximately $6.4 million, factoring in a $1.7 million of deemed dividends resulting from warrant repricing and a $0.3 million unrealized loss on securities, compared to a $4.4 million loss in the prior year.</font></div></div>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Core EBITDA:</font><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> Core EBITDA loss was $1.6 million in Q3 2024 from $0.6 million in Q3 2023, although positive Core EBITDA for the nine months of 2024 increased to $0.6 million due to expanded Bitcoin operations. (</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Core EBITDA is a non-GAAP financial measure, and a reconciliation of Core EBITDA to net loss can be found below)</font><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">CFO commentary</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#121512;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Richard Russell, CFO of LM Funding, stated, &#34;We closed the quarter with approximately $14.9 million in cash and Bitcoin. With the recent rapid increase in BTC prices above $87,000, we are extremely optimistic about the financial prospects of Bitcoin and our business outlook.&#34;</font></p>
  <p style="margin-left:3.333%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Investor Conference Call</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">LM Funding will host a conference call today, November 13, 2024, at 11:00 A.M. Eastern Time to discuss the Company&#x2019;s financial results for the quarter ended September 30, 2024, as well as the Company&#x2019;s corporate progress and other developments.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">The conference call will be available via telephone by dialing toll-free +1 888-506-0062 for U.S. callers or +1 973-528-0011 for international callers and entering access code 424451. A webcast of the call may be accessed at </font><font><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">https://www.webcaster4.com/Webcast/Page/2917/51557</font></font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> or on the investor relations section of the company&#x2019;s website, </font><font><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">https://www.lmfunding.com/investors/news-events/ir-calendar</font></font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></p>

  <div style="padding-top:0.5in;z-index:-3;min-height:0.5in;position:relative;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Exhibit 99.1</font></p></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">A webcast replay will be available on the investor relations section of the company&#x2019;s website at </font><font><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">https://www.lmfunding.com/investors/news-events/ir-calendar</font></font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> through November 13, 2025. A telephone replay of the call will be available approximately one hour following the call, through November 27, 2024, and can be accessed by dialing 877-481-4010 for U.S. callers or +1 919-882-2331 for international callers and entering access code 51557.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">About LM Funding America</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">LM Funding America, Inc., (Nasdaq: LMFA) and its subsidiaries are a cryptocurrency mining business that commenced Bitcoin mining operations in September 2022. The Company also operates a technology-based specialty finance company that provides funding to nonprofit community associations (Associations) primarily located in the state of Florida, as well as in the states of Washington, Colorado, and Illinois, by funding a certain portion of the Associations' rights to delinquent accounts that are selected by the Associations arising from unpaid Association assessments.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Forward-Looking Statements</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">This press release may contain forward-looking statements made pursuant to the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. Forward-looking statements are not guarantees of future results and conditions but rather are subject to various risks and uncertainties. Some of these risks and uncertainties are identified in the Company's most recent Annual Report on Form 10-K and its other filings with the SEC, which are available at </font><font><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">www.sec.gov</font></font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">.   <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">NON-GAAP FINANCIAL INFORMATION (unaudited)</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">Our reported results are presented in accordance with U.S. generally accepted accounting principles (&#x201c;GAAP&#x201d;). We also disclose  Earnings before Interest, Tax, Depreciation and Amortization (&#34;EBITDA&#34;) and Core Earnings before Interest, Tax, Depreciation and Amortization (&#34;Core EBITDA&#34;) which adjusts for unrealized loss on investment and equity securities, impairment loss on mined digital assets, impairment of long-lived assets, impairment of prepaid hosting deposits, contract termination costs and stock compensation expense and option expense, all of which are non-GAAP financial measures. We believe these non-GAAP financial measures are useful to investors because they are widely accepted industry measures used by analysts and investors to compare the operating performance of Bitcoin miners.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">The following tables reconcile net loss, which we believe is the most comparable GAAP measure, to EBITDA and Core EBITDA:</font></p>
